const config = {
    layers: [
        { type: LayerType.Input,  inputs: 11, units: 11 }, //11 features
        { type: LayerType.Hidden, inputs: 11, units: 5, functions: Array(5).fill('ReLU') },

        { type: LayerType.Final, inputs: 5, units: 1, functions: ['Linear'] } // 1 saída contínua
    ],

};
